1
1518949864
@ kakiuchis
Edited at 2018-04-03
Heroku deployment of image recognition application made with Python (Flask) uses heroku.yml for OpenCV installation
Python
Heroku
Flask
OpenCV
Symptom

I made an image recognition application with Flask.
At first glance Heroku deployment seems to have worked.
But the screen below.

https://gyazo.com/98adba5a2f96966c8e9685b604d4e236

Check the log.

  app [web.1]: File "/app/.heroku/python/lib/python3.6/site-packages/cv2/__init__.py", line 4, in <module>
 app [web.1]: from. cv2 import *
 app [web.1]: ImportError: libSM.so.6: can not open shared object file: No such file or directory
 app [web.1]: [4] [INFO] Shutting down: Master
 app [web.1]: [4] [INFO] Reason: Worker failed to boot.
 heroku [web.1]: Process exited with status 3
 heroku [web.1]: State changed from up to crashed
 heroku [router]: at = error code = H10 desc = "App crashed" method = GET path = "/" host = xxxx.herokuapp.com request_id = xxxxx - xxxx - xxxx - xxxx - xxxxxxxx fwd = "xx.xxx. xx.xx "dyno = connect = service = status = 503 bytes = protocol = https

What is this?
Cause of error

If something like import cv2 commented out error resolution.
※ Well, of course there is no cv2 so python is working. .
That is, import cv2 is the cause.
It seems that you could not install openCV in Heroku environment.
How to install OpenCV on Heroku in

There is opencv-python in the requirements.txt properly. .
requirements.txt

  Flask == 0.12
 gunicorn == 19.7.1
 Jinja 2 == 2.9.4
 numpy == 1.14.1
 opencv-python == 3.4.0.12
 tensorflow == 1.5.0

After examining various things, it seems that you have to install OpenCV on Heroku using Docker or heroku.yml .
Do not know Docker, do it at heroku.yml!

Create the following file.
heroku.yml

  build :
   languages :
     - python
   packages :
     - libopencv-dev
 run :
   web : gunicorn web: app - log - file = -

※ runtime.txt are OK with runtime.txt , Procfile , requirement.txt is. .

so,

  $ git add - A
 $ git commit -m "heroku.yml do it"
 $ heroku stack: set container
 $ git push heroku master

Then Zukozo openCV will come to Heroku!
It goes together all the time!
1
Toot
1518949864
Shinku Kakiuchi @ kakiuchis ITPM Corporation

    症状
    エラーの原因
    でどうやってOpenCVをHerokuにインストールするのか
    Docker知らんし、heroku.ymlでやろう！

import os

import sys



path = '/home/RohitDhankar/python_pdf_parsing/' 

if path not in sys.path:
    
    sys.path.append(path)

# This file contains the WSGI configuration required to serve up your
# web application at http://www.digitalcognition.co.in/
# It works by setting the variable 'application' to a WSGI handler of some
# description.
#

# +++++++++++ GENERAL DEBUGGING TIPS +++++++++++
# getting imports and sys.path right can be fiddly!
# We've tried to collect some general tips here:
# https://www.pythonanywhere.com/wiki/DebuggingImportError


# +++++++++++ HELLO WORLD +++++++++++
# A little pure-wsgi hello world we've cooked up, just
# to prove everything works.  You should delete this
# code to get your own working.


HELLO_WORLD = """<html>
<head>
    <title>Python Anywhere hosted web application</title>
</head>
<body>
<h1>Hello, World!</h1>
<p>
    This is the default welcome page for a
    <a href="https://www.pythonanywhere.com/">PythonAnywhere</a>
    hosted web application.
</p>
<p>
    Find out more about how to configure your own web application
    by visiting the <a href="https://www.pythonanywhere.com/web_app_setup/">web app setup</a> page
</p>
</body>
</html>"""


def application(environ, start_response):
    if environ.get('PATH_INFO') == '/':
        status = '200 OK'
        content = HELLO_WORLD
    else:
        status = '404 NOT FOUND'
        content = 'Page not found.'
    response_headers = [('Content-Type', 'text/html'), ('Content-Length', str(len(content)))]
    start_response(status, response_headers)
    yield content.encode('utf8')

#Django Database Indexing --- Creating Index on ROWS or Model Fields 

In Django ORM --- Indexes are created automatically on PRIMARY Keys and FOREIGN Keys 
# MAIN ---- Indexing ---- https://docs.djangoproject.com/en/1.10/topics/db/optimization/

# https://www.djangorocks.com/snippets/indexing-your-django-models.html

SO ANswer --- 
This is not really django specific; more to do with databases. 
You add indexes on columns when you want to speed up searches on that column.
Typically, only the primary key is indexed by the database. 
This means look ups using the primary key are optimized.
If you do a lot of lookups on a secondary column, consider adding 
an index to that column to speed things up.

Keep in mind, like most problems of scale, these only apply if you
 have a statistically large number of rows (10,000 is not large).
Additionally, every time you do an insert, indexes need to be updated. 
So be careful on which column you add indexes.

As always, you can only optimize what you can measure - so use 
the EXPLAIN statement and your database logs (especially any slow query logs) 
to find out where indexes can be useful.

Relative linking uses a reference relative to the current file. For example if you
have an image in /images or /m/images and your html is in either / or /m, you can
create the following <img> tag to reference this file:
<img src="images/someimage.jpg">


 Absolute linking creates two different links:
<img src="/images/someimage.jpg">
or
<img src="/m/images/someimage.jpg">

# TBD ---- Veri ---------------------------------------------------------------
# Getting Multiple Images from Product odel to Template for LightBox 
def get_first_image(self):
        images = self.productimage_set.all()
        if images.count() == 0:
            return None
        first_image = images[0]
        return first_image

    def get_more_images(self):
        return self.productimage_set.all()[1:]

    def has_multiple_images(self):
        return self.productimage_set.count() > 1

        sale_price = models.DecimalField(decimal_places=2, max_digits=20,blank=True, null=True)#SELLING_PRICE-Not_DIWALI SALE 
        BHK_Count = models.IntegerField(null=True, blank=True) #refer none == unlimited amount # DHANKAR - PROP
        Property_Area_SqFt = models.IntegerField(blank=True, null=True) # DHANKAR - PROP
        Kitchen_Attached = models.BooleanField(default=True)
        BathRoom_Attached = models.BooleanField(default=True)
        Address_Line1_House_Flat_NO = models.TextField(blank=True, null=True) # DHANKAR - PROP
        Address_Line2_StreetName = models.TextField(blank=True, null=True) # DHANKAR - PROP
        Address_Line3_Locality_Sector_Name = models.TextField(blank=True, null=True) # DHANKAR - PROP
        Address_Line4_City_Town_Name = models.TextField(blank=True, null=True) # DHANKAR - PROP
        Address_Line5_StateName = models.TextField(blank=True, null=True) # DHANKAR - PROP
        Address_Line6_PinCode = models.TextField(blank=True, null=True) # DHANKAR - PROP
        Address_Line7_ProminentLandmark = models.TextField(blank=True, null=True) # DHANKAR - PROP
        Address_Line8_TeleContact = models.TextField(blank=True, null=True) # DHANKAR - PROP
        Owner_Contact_Person_Name = models.TextField(blank=True, null=True) # DHANKAR - PROP
        active = models.BooleanField(default=True)
        categories = models.ManyToManyField('Category', blank=True)  # MANY TO MANY FIELD --- Like STYLE in TAP Above 
        default = models.ForeignKey('Category', related_name='default_category', null=True, blank=True)

class PROPS_PRINT_View(ListView): #------------------------------------------------- CHANGE VIEW NAME 
    
    model =PVh                       #---------------------------------------------- CHANGE MODEL HERE 
    template_name = 'All_Prop_Display.html' #-------------------------------------- CHANGE TEMPLATE NAME
    
    paginate_by = 20
        
    def get_context_data(self, **kwargs):
        context = super(PROPS_PRINT_View, self).get_context_data(**kwargs) 
        list_props = PVh.objects.all() #-------------------------------------------- CHANGE MODEL HERE 
        #list_Tweets = Tw0.objects.filter(text='')
        paginator = Paginator(list_props, self.paginate_by)

        page = self.request.GET.get('page')

        try:
            file_TweetsPage = paginator.page(page)
        except PageNotAnInteger:
            file_TweetsPage = paginator.page(1)
        except EmptyPage:
            file_TweetsPage = paginator.page(paginator.num_pages)

        context['list_props'] = file_TweetsPage
        return context

# Main Search All Models --------------------------------DONT CHANGE ---- JUST ADD MODELS BELOW 
def search(request):
    if 'q' in request.GET and request.GET['q']:
        q = request.GET['q']
        Prop_0 = PVh.objects.filter(Q(propname__icontains=q)|
                                  Q(pricesale__icontains=q)|  
                                    Q(pricerental__icontains=q)|  
                                    Q(address_line4_zonename__icontains=q)|
                                    Q(address_line5_cityname__icontains=q)|
                                    Q(address_line3_localityname__icontains=q)
                                  )    
        
        #To be Used when Searching with One Query In More Than 1 DataTable , Models 
        #
        Prop_1 = Product.objects.filter(Q(title__icontains=q)|
                                  Q(description__icontains=q)|  
                                  Q(Rental_price__icontains=q)|  
                                  Q(sale_price__icontains=q)|
                                  Q(BHK_Count__icontains=q)|
                                  Q(Property_Area_SqFt__icontains=q)|
                                  Q(Address_Line1_House_Flat_NO__icontains=q)|
                                  Q(Address_Line2_StreetName__icontains=q)|
                                  Q(Address_Line3_Locality_Sector_Name__icontains=q)|
                                  Q(Address_Line4_City_Town_Name__icontains=q)|
                                  Q(Address_Line5_StateName__icontains=q)|
                                  Q(Address_Line6_PinCode__icontains=q)|           
                                  Q(Address_Line7_ProminentLandmark__icontains=q)
                                  )    
       
      
        
        return render(request, 'search_results.html',
            {'Prop_0': Prop_0,'Prop_1': Prop_1, 'query': q})
            
    else:
        return HttpResponse('Please submit a search term for Property Search.')

# Create your views here.
def home(request):
	title = 'Sign Up Now'

	featured_image = ProductFeatured.objects.filter(active=True).order_by("?").first()

	form = SignUpForm(request.POST or None)
	context = {
		"title": title,
		"form": form,
		"featured_image":featured_image,
	}


	if form.is_valid():
		#form.save()
		#print request.POST['email'] #not recommended
		instance = form.save(commit=False)

		full_name = form.cleaned_data.get("full_name")
		if not full_name:
			full_name = "New full name"
		instance.full_name = full_name
		# if not instance.full_name:
		# 	instance.full_name = "Justin"
		instance.save()
		context = {
			"title": "Thank you"
		}

	if request.user.is_authenticated() and request.user.is_staff:
		#print(SignUp.objects.all())
		# i = 1
		# for instance in SignUp.objects.all():
		# 	print(i)
		# 	print(instance.full_name)
		# 	i += 1

		queryset = SignUp.objects.all().order_by('-timestamp') #.filter(full_name__iexact="Justin")
		#print(SignUp.objects.all().order_by('-timestamp').filter(full_name__iexact="Justin").count())
		context = {
			"queryset": queryset
		}

	return render(request, "home.html", context)



def contact(request):
	title = 'Contact Us'
	title_align_center = True
	form = ContactForm(request.POST or None)
	if form.is_valid():
		# for key, value in form.cleaned_data.iteritems():
		# 	print key, value
		# 	#print form.cleaned_data.get(key)
		form_email = form.cleaned_data.get("email")
		form_message = form.cleaned_data.get("message")
		form_full_name = form.cleaned_data.get("full_name")
		# print email, message, full_name
		subject = 'Site contact form'
		from_email = settings.EMAIL_HOST_USER
		to_email = [from_email, 'youotheremail@email.com']
		contact_message = "%s: %s via %s"%( 
				form_full_name, 
				form_message, 
				form_email)
		some_html_message = """
		<h1>hello</h1>
		"""
		send_mail(subject, 
				contact_message, 
				from_email, 
				to_email, 
				html_message=some_html_message,
				fail_silently=True)

	context = {
		"form": form,
		"title": title,
		"title_align_center": title_align_center,
	}
	return render(request, "forms.html", context)

class CategoryListView(ListView):
        model = Category
        queryset = Category.objects.all()
        template_name = "products/product_list.html" # Its Called - CategoryListView --- But has PRODUCT_LIST Template HMMMM

class CategoryListViewHome(ListView):
        model = Category
        queryset = Category.objects.all()
        template_name = "home.html" # This was done to Display All Categories on Homepage --- 09 SEP 

        
class CategoryDetailView(DetailView):
        model = Category

        def get_context_data(self, *args, **kwargs):
                context = super(CategoryDetailView, self).get_context_data(*args, **kwargs)
                obj = self.get_object()
                product_set = obj.product_set.all()
                default_products = obj.default_category.all()
                products = ( product_set | default_products ).distinct()
                context["products"] = products
                return context



class VariationListView(StaffRequiredMixin,ListView):
        model = Variation
        queryset = Variation.objects.all()

        def get_context_data(self, *args, **kwargs):
            context = super(VariationListView, self).get_context_data(*args, **kwargs)
            context["formset"] = VariationInventoryFormSet(queryset=self.get_queryset())
            return context

        def get_queryset(self, *args, **kwargs):
            product_pk = self.kwargs.get("pk")
            if product_pk:
                product = get_object_or_404(Product, pk=product_pk)
                queryset = Variation.objects.filter(product=product)
            return queryset

        def post(self, request, *args, **kwargs):
            #
            formset = VariationInventoryFormSet(request.POST, request.FILES)
            #print request.POST
            if formset.is_valid():
                formset.save(commit=False)
                for form in formset:
                    new_item = form.save(commit=False)
                    #if new_item.title:
                    product_pk = self.kwargs.get("pk")
                    product = get_object_or_404(Product, pk=product_pk)
                    new_item.product = product
                    new_item.save()

                messages.success(request, "Your inventory and pricing has been updated.")
                return redirect("products")
            raise Http404



class ProductListView(ListView):
        model = Product
        queryset = Product.objects.all()

        def get_context_data(self, *args, **kwargs):
                context = super(ProductListView, self).get_context_data(*args, **kwargs)
                context["now"] = timezone.now()
                context["query"] = self.request.GET.get("q") #None
                return context

        def get_queryset(self, *args, **kwargs):
                qs = super(ProductListView, self).get_queryset(*args, **kwargs)
                query = self.request.GET.get("q")
                if query:
                    qs = self.model.objects.filter(
                        Q(title__icontains=query) |
                        Q(description__icontains=query)
                        )
                    try:
                        qs2 = self.model.objects.filter(
                            Q(price=query)
                        )
                        qs = (qs | qs2).distinct()
                    except:
                        pass
                return qs

class ProductDetailView(DetailView):
        model = Product
        #template_name = "product.html"
        #template_name = "<appname>/<modelname>_detail.html"
        def get_context_data(self, *args, **kwargs):
                context = super(ProductDetailView, self).get_context_data(*args, **kwargs)
                instance = self.get_object()
                #order_by("-title")
                #order_by("title") # Dhankar _TBD
                context["related"] = sorted(Product.objects.get_related(instance)[:6], key= lambda x: random.random())#Dhankar_3
                #context["related"] = sorted(Product.objects.get_related(instance)[:5], key= lambda x: random.random())
                return context


def product_detail_view_func(request, id):
        #product_instance = Product.objects.get(id=id)
        product_instance = get_object_or_404(Product, id=id)
        try:
            product_instance = Product.objects.get(id=id)
        except Product.DoesNotExist:
            raise Http404
        except:
            raise Http404

        template = "products/product_detail.html"
        context = {	
            "object": product_instance
        }
        return render(request, template, context)

def Tw3_detail_view_func(request, id):
        #product_instance = Product.objects.get(id=id)
        Tw3_instance = get_object_or_404(Tw3, id=id)
        try:
            Tw3_instance = Tw3.objects.get(id=id)

            raise Http404
        except:
            raise Http404

        template = "products/Tw3_detail.html"

                                  Q(Address_Line2_StreetName__icontains=q)|
                                  Q(Address_Line3_Locality_Sector_Name__icontains=q)|
                                  Q(Address_Line4_City_Town_Name__icontains=q)|
                                  Q(Address_Line5_StateName__icontains=q)|
                                  Q(Address_Line6_PinCode__icontains=q)|           
                                  Q(Address_Line7_ProminentLandmark__icontains=q)
                                  )    
       
      
        
        return render(request, 'search_results.html',
            {'Prop_0': Prop_0,'Prop_1': Prop_1, 'query': q})
            
    else:
        return HttpResponse('Please submit a search term for Property Search.')

def home(request):
	title = 'Sign Up Now'

	featured_image = ProductFeatured.objects.filter(active=True).order_by("?").first()

	form = SignUpForm(request.POST or None)
	context = {
		"title": title,
		"form": form,
		"featured_image":featured_image,
	}


	if form.is_valid():
		#form.save()
		#print request.POST['email'] #not recommended
		instance = form.save(commit=False)

		full_name = form.cleaned_data.get("full_name")
		if not full_name:
			full_name = "New full name"
		instance.full_name = full_name
		# if not instance.full_name:
		# 	instance.full_name = "Justin"
		instance.save()
		context = {
			"title": "Thank you"
		}

	if request.user.is_authenticated() and request.user.is_staff:
		#print(SignUp.objects.all())
		# i = 1
		# for instance in SignUp.objects.all():
		# 	print(i)
		# 	print(instance.full_name)
		# 	i += 1

		queryset = SignUp.objects.all().order_by('-timestamp') #.filter(full_name__iexact="Justin")
		#print(SignUp.objects.all().order_by('-timestamp').filter(full_name__iexact="Justin").count())
		context = {
			"queryset": queryset
		}

	return render(request, "home.html", context)



def contact(request):
	title = 'Contact Us'
	title_align_center = True
	form = ContactForm(request.POST or None)
	if form.is_valid():
		# for key, value in form.cleaned_data.iteritems():
		# 	print key, value
		# 	#print form.cleaned_data.get(key)
		form_email = form.cleaned_data.get("email")
		form_message = form.cleaned_data.get("message")
		form_full_name = form.cleaned_data.get("full_name")
		# print email, message, full_name
		subject = 'Site contact form'
		from_email = settings.EMAIL_HOST_USER
		to_email = [from_email, 'youotheremail@email.com']
		contact_message = "%s: %s via %s"%( 
				form_full_name, 
				form_message, 
				form_email)
		some_html_message = """
		<h1>hello</h1>
		"""
		send_mail(subject, 
				contact_message, 
				from_email, 
				to_email, 
				html_message=some_html_message,
				fail_silently=True)

	context = {
		"form": form,
		"title": title,
		"title_align_center": title_align_center,
	}
	return render(request, "forms.html", context)

class CategoryListView(ListView):
        model = Category
        queryset = Category.objects.all()
        template_name = "products/product_list.html" # Its Called - CategoryListView --- But has PRODUCT_LIST Template HMMMM

class CategoryListViewHome(ListView):
        model = Category
        queryset = Category.objects.all()
        template_name = "home.html" # This was done to Display All Categories on Homepage --- 09 SEP 

        
class CategoryDetailView(DetailView):
        model = Category

        def get_context_data(self, *args, **kwargs):
                context = super(CategoryDetailView, self).get_context_data(*args, **kwargs)
                obj = self.get_object()
                product_set = obj.product_set.all()
                default_products = obj.default_category.all()
                products = ( product_set | default_products ).distinct()
                context["products"] = products
                return context



class VariationListView(StaffRequiredMixin,ListView):
        model = Variation
        queryset = Variation.objects.all()

        def get_context_data(self, *args, **kwargs):
            context = super(VariationListView, self).get_context_data(*args, **kwargs)
            context["formset"] = VariationInventoryFormSet(queryset=self.get_queryset())
            return context

        def get_queryset(self, *args, **kwargs):
            product_pk = self.kwargs.get("pk")
            if product_pk:
                product = get_object_or_404(Product, pk=product_pk)
                queryset = Variation.objects.filter(product=product)
            return queryset

        def post(self, request, *args, **kwargs):
            #
            formset = VariationInventoryFormSet(request.POST, request.FILES)
            #print request.POST
            if formset.is_valid():
                formset.save(commit=False)
                for form in formset:
                    new_item = form.save(commit=False)
                    #if new_item.title:
                    product_pk = self.kwargs.get("pk")
                    product = get_object_or_404(Product, pk=product_pk)
                    new_item.product = product
                    new_item.save()

                messages.success(request, "Your inventory and pricing has been updated.")
                return redirect("products")
            raise Http404

def contact1(request):
    if request.method == 'POST':
        form = ImageUploadForm(request.POST, request.FILES)
        if form.is_valid():
            product_pk = Product.kwargs.get("pk") # Own Addition - class VariationListView ---ABOVE - 14 SEP
            m = ProductImage.objects.get(pk="product_pk") # here Changed MODEL NAME TO OWN == "ProductImage" from ExampleModel
            m.image = form.cleaned_data['image']
            m.save()
            return HttpResponse('image upload success')
        return HttpResponseForbidden('allowed only via POST')
    return render(request, "contact1.html", {})

class ProductListView(ListView):
        model = Product
        queryset = Product.objects.all()

        def get_context_data(self, *args, **kwargs):
                context = super(ProductListView, self).get_context_data(*args, **kwargs)
                context["now"] = timezone.now()
                context["query"] = self.request.GET.get("q") #None
                return context

        def get_queryset(self, *args, **kwargs):
                qs = super(ProductListView, self).get_queryset(*args, **kwargs)
                query = self.request.GET.get("q")
                if query:
                    qs = self.model.objects.filter(
                        Q(title__icontains=query) |
                        Q(description__icontains=query)
                        )
                    try:
                        qs2 = self.model.objects.filter(
                            Q(price=query)
                        )
                        qs = (qs | qs2).distinct()
                    except:
                        pass
                return qs

class ProductDetailView(DetailView):
        model = Product
        #template_name = "product.html"
        #template_name = "<appname>/<modelname>_detail.html"
        def get_context_data(self, *args, **kwargs):
                context = super(ProductDetailView, self).get_context_data(*args, **kwargs)
                instance = self.get_object()
                #order_by("-title")
                #order_by("title") # Dhankar _TBD
                context["related"] = sorted(Product.objects.get_related(instance)[:6], key= lambda x: random.random())#Dhankar_3
                #context["related"] = sorted(Product.objects.get_related(instance)[:5], key= lambda x: random.random())
                return context


def product_detail_view_func(request, id):
        #product_instance = Product.objects.get(id=id)
        product_instance = get_object_or_404(Product, id=id)
        try:
            product_instance = Product.objects.get(id=id)
        except Product.DoesNotExist:
            raise Http404
        except:
            raise Http404

        template = "products/product_detail.html"
        context = {	
            "object": product_instance
        }
        return render(request, template, context)

---------------

James McIntosh - and other friends here who might believe that Data Scientist is some kind of lofty title and its way too much "gas" and not really something practical or to do with vocational data analysis - well consider this - https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Data_science#Data_scientist ....

"Data scientists use their data and analytical ability to find and interpret rich data sources; manage large amounts of data despite hardware, software, and bandwidth constraints,"

The First line itself - who would have had such a job description say a decade back ---- why would there be need of such data crunching back then , so this is surely an interesting discussion - but what needs to be kept upmost in mind is , that its an evolving field of work . 

If i have access to 30 Terra Bytes of Data in an established Hadoop Data lake on some really stable and high end stable systems - would i not be able to run analysis on manageable chunks of data - some sort of batch processing - well maybe yes ...but then would i be a data scientist - probably not - not as per the line quoted above ....n thats just the tip of the iceberg ...

def contact(request):
    #title = 'Contact Us'
	#title_align_center = True
	form = ContactForm(request.POST or None)
	if form.is_valid():
		#for key, value in form.cleaned_data.iteritems():
		 	#print key, value
		 	#print form.cleaned_data.get(key)
            
        form_email = form.cleaned_data.get("email")
        form_message = form.cleaned_data.get("message")
        form_full_name = form.cleaned_data.get("full_name")

        # print email, message, full_name
        subject = 'Site contact form'
        from_email = settings.EMAIL_HOST_USER
        to_email = [from_email, 'rohit.dhankar@strategic-leadership-llc-india.com']
        contact_message = "%s: %s via %s"%( 
                form_full_name, 
                form_message, 
                form_email)
        some_html_message = """
        <h1>Hi There , Thanks for showing interest in Data Science India - we shall get back to you shortly.</h1>
        """
        send_mail(subject, 
                contact_message, 
                from_email, 
                to_email, 
                html_message=some_html_message,
                fail_silently=False)

    context = {
        "form": form,
        "title": title,
        "title_align_center": title_align_center,
    }
    return render(request, "forms.html", context)

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
    <head>
        <meta charset="utf-8">
        <title>D32 Page Template</title>
        <script src="//d3js.org/d3.v3.min.js"></script>
        
    </head>
    <body>
        
        <script type="text/javascript">
            // Your beautiful D3 code will go here
            //
            // #######
            
            
              var dataArray =[5,11,14,17,19,23,40,50,55];
            
              var width = 600;
              var height = 600;
            
              var widthScale = d3.scale.linear()
                          .domain([0,60])
                          .range([0,width]);
                                  
              var color = d3.scale.linear()
                          .domain([0,60])
                          .range(["yellow","green"]);
                           
                           // The - d3.scale.linear - will take MIN -0[Pure RED] and MAX -60[Pure BLUE]
            
              var axis = d3.svg.axis()
                          .ticks(5)
                          .scale(widthScale);  
                                  
              var canvas = d3.select("body")
                      .append("svg")
                      .attr("width",width) // width - taken up from here into a WIDTH var ...
                      .attr("height",height) // height - taken up from here into a HEIGHT var ...
                      .append("g") // g - means Group 
                      .attr("transform","translate(20,70)");
                      
                     
            
              var bars = canvas.selectAll("rect")
                      .data(dataArray)
                      .enter() 
                        .append("rect")
                        .attr("width",function(d) {return widthScale(d); }) 
                        .attr("height",30)
                        .attr("fill",function(d) {return color(d)}) 
                        .attr("y", function(d,i){return i * 50});
            
             canvas.append("g")
                 .attr("transform","translate(0,500)")
                 .call(axis);
            
            
                   // "d" variable passed into the ---accessor functions--- stands for "datum"
      // here - function(d) is same as function(i) the used to iterate - 
      // i will iterate through the values in -- .enter - which are values of dataArray
      // i/d will assign the attr("width") of the Rectangle  with diff variable values from dataArray . 
            // The function(d,i) will return - i from within the - d - thus First i ==20 , next i==40 and 50 
            

            
             // D3 code Above this --
            //
            // #######
            
            
            
            
            
            
            </script>
    </body>
</html>

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
    <head>
        <meta charset="utf-8">
        <title>D32 Page Template</title>
        <script src="//d3js.org/d3.v3.min.js"></script>
        
    </head>
    <body>
